idle = {
	male = {
		default = { head = "idle_entry" torso = "idle_entry" }

		AI_idle_infant = {
			animation = { head = "idle_entry" torso = "idleInfant_entry" }
			weight = {
				base = 0
				modifier = {
					add = 100
					scope:age <= 5
				}
			}
		}

		AI_idle_child = {
			animation = { head = "idle_entry" torso = "idleInfant_entry" }
			weight = {
				base = 0
				modifier = {
					add = 100
					always = no #scope:age <= 9
				}
			}
		}

		AI_idle_basic = {
			animation = { head = "idle_entry" torso = "idle_entry" }
			weight = {
				base = 0
				modifier = {
					add = 99
					#scope:age >= 10
					scope:current_weight <= 75
				}
			}
		}

		AI_idle_fat = {
			animation = { head = "idle_entry" torso = "idleFat_entry" }
			weight = {
				base = 0
				modifier = {
					add = 100
					#scope:age >= 10
					scope:current_weight >= 75
				}
			}
		}

		AI_honorable = {
			animation = { head = "AI_honorable_entry" torso = "AI_honorable_entry" }
			weight = {
				base = 0
				# Score set to 100 + the actual ai_value score (will range from 150 to 200)
				modifier = {
					add = {
						value = 100
						add = scope:ai_honor
					}
					#scope:age >= 10
					scope:ai_honor >= max_positive_honor
					scope:current_weight <= 50
					NOT = { portrait_has_trait_trigger = { TRAIT = dwarf } }
					NOT = { portrait_has_trait_trigger = { TRAIT = pregnant } }
					portrait_wear_armor_trigger = no
					portrait_mena_clothing_trigger = no
				}
			}
		}

		AI_dishonorable = {
			animation = { head = "AI_dishonorable_entry" torso = "AI_dishonorable_entry" }
			weight = {
				base = 0
				# Score set to 100 + the inverse of the negative ai_value score (will range from 150 to 200)
				modifier = {
					add = {
						value = 100
						add = {
							value = ai_honor
							multiply = -1
						}
					}
					#scope:age >= 10
					scope:ai_honor <= max_negative_honor
					scope:current_weight <= 20
					NOT = { portrait_has_trait_trigger = { TRAIT = dwarf } }
					NOT = { portrait_has_trait_trigger = { TRAIT = pregnant } }
					portrait_wear_armor_trigger = no
					portrait_mena_clothing_trigger = no                
				}
			}
			portrait_modifier = {							# Triggered portrait modifier for when this animation is picked. The first one satisfying the trigger will be picked.
				animations = AI_dishonorable_decal				# One or multiple portrait modifier overrides
			}
		}

# misc_pregnantSerious_entry (above) is for characeters with negative traits
#
# misc_pregnant_entry (below) is for characters with positive traits
#
# we had to put pregnant triggers all the way down here because we need to prioritize playing misc_pregnantSerious_entry. hence, you can find misc_pregnantSerious_entry above.
# 

		AI_pregnant_dwarf_or_armor = {
			animation = { head = "misc_pregnant_entry" torso = "misc_pregnantFat_entry" }
			weight = {
				base = 0
				modifier = {
					add = 100
					OR = {
						portrait_has_trait_trigger = { TRAIT = dwarf }
						portrait_wear_armor_trigger = yes
					}
					portrait_has_trait_trigger = { TRAIT = pregnant }
				}
			}
		}

		AI_pregnant = {
			animation = { head = "misc_pregnant_entry" torso = "misc_pregnant_entry" }
			weight = {
				base = 0
				modifier = {
					add = 100
					portrait_has_trait_trigger = { TRAIT = pregnant }
					NOT = { portrait_has_trait_trigger = { TRAIT = dwarf } }
				}
			}
		}
    }
	boy = male
	female = male
	girl = male
}

anger = {
	male = {
		default = { head = "emotion_angry_entry" torso = "emotion_angry_entry" }
		emotion_angry_hunchbacked = {
			animation = { head = "idle_entry" torso = "idle_entry" }
			weight = {
				base = 0
				modifier = {
					add = 110
					portrait_has_trait_trigger = { TRAIT = hunchbacked }
				}
			}
		}

		emotion_angry_infant = {
			animation = { head = "idle" torso = "idleInfant_entry" }

			weight = {
				base = 0

				modifier = {
					add = 100
					scope:age <= 5
				}
			}
		}

		emotion_angry_child = {
			animation = { head = "idle_entry" torso = "idle_entry" }

			weight = {
				base = 0

				modifier = {
					add = 100
					always = no #scope:age <= 9

				}
			}
		}

		emotion_angry = {
			animation = { head = "emotion_angry_entry" torso = "emotion_angry_entry" }

			weight = {
				base = 0

				modifier = {
					add = 100
					AND = {
						scope:current_weight < 60
						NOT = { portrait_has_trait_trigger = { TRAIT = dwarf } }
						NOT = { portrait_has_trait_trigger = { TRAIT = pregnant } }                        
					}
				}
			}

			portrait_modifier = {							# Triggered portrait modifier for when this animation is picked. The first one satisfying the trigger will be picked.
				animations = emotion_angry_decal
			}
		}

		emotion_angry_fat = {
			animation = { head = "emotion_angryFat_entry" torso = "emotion_angryFat_entry" }

			weight = {
				base = 0

				modifier = {
					add = 100
					AND = {
						scope:current_weight > 60
						NOT = { portrait_has_trait_trigger = { TRAIT = dwarf } }
						NOT = { portrait_has_trait_trigger = { TRAIT = pregnant } }
					}

		portrait_modifier = { # Equipped
			trigger = {
				any_equipped_character_artifact = { artifact_type = dagger }
			}
			animations_props = artifact_dagger_equipped_prop
			animations = AI_vengeful_decal
		}

		portrait_modifier = { # Norse
			trigger = {
				NOT = {	any_equipped_character_artifact = { artifact_type = dagger } }
				culture = { has_clothing_gfx = northern_clothing_gfx }
			}
			animations_props = spymaster_fp1_prop
			animations = AI_vengeful_decal
		}

		portrait_modifier = { # Iberian
			trigger = {
				NOT = {	any_equipped_character_artifact = { artifact_type = dagger } }
				culture = {
					OR = {
						has_clothing_gfx = iberian_christian_clothing_gfx
						has_clothing_gfx = iberian_muslim_clothing_gfx
					}
				}
			}
			animations_props = spymaster_fp2_prop

			}
			animations_props = spymaster_mena_prop
			animations = AI_vengeful_decal
		}

		portrait_modifier = { # Indian
			trigger = {
				NOT = {
					any_equipped_character_artifact = { artifact_type = dagger }
				}
				culture = {
					OR = {
						has_clothing_gfx = african_clothing_gfx
						has_clothing_gfx = indian_clothing_gfx

					}
				}
			}
			animations_props = spymaster_indian_prop
			animations = AI_vengeful_decal
		}

				}
				dagger_unique_gfx_trigger = no
			}
			animations_props = spymaster_prop
			animations = AI_vengeful_decal
		}
	}

sword_coup_degrace = {
	male = { 
		default = { head = "sword_coup_degrace_entry" torso = "sword_coup_degrace_entry" } 

		portrait_modifier = { # Norse
			trigger = {
				culture = { has_clothing_gfx = northern_clothing_gfx }
			}			
			animations_props = marshal_fp1_prop
			animations = AI_vengeful_decal
		}

		portrait_modifier = { # Iberian Christian
			trigger = {
				culture = { has_clothing_gfx = iberian_christian_clothing_gfx }
			}
			animations_props = marshal_fp2_christian_prop
			animations = AI_vengeful_decal
		}

		portrait_modifier = { # Iberian Muslim
			trigger = {
				culture = { has_clothing_gfx = iberian_muslim_clothing_gfx }
			}
			animations_props = marshal_fp2_muslim_prop
			animations = AI_vengeful_decal
		}

		portrait_modifier = { # Steppe
			trigger = {
				culture = { has_clothing_gfx = mongol_clothing_gfx }
			}			
			animations_props = artisan_sword_steppe_prop
			animations = AI_vengeful_decal
		}

		portrait_modifier = { # Mediterranean
			trigger = {
				culture = { has_clothing_gfx = byzantine_clothing_gfx }
			}			
			animations_props = artisan_sword_byzantine_prop
			animations = AI_vengeful_decal
		}

		portrait_modifier = { # Indian
			trigger = {
				culture = { has_clothing_gfx = indian_clothing_gfx }
			}			
			animations_props = artisan_sword_indian_prop
			animations = AI_vengeful_decal
		}

		portrait_modifier = { # MENA
			trigger = {
				culture = {
					OR = {
						has_clothing_gfx = african_clothing_gfx
						has_clothing_gfx = mena_clothing_gfx
					}
				}
			}			
			animations_props = artisan_sword_mena_prop
			animations = AI_vengeful_decal
		}

		portrait_modifier = { # Western
			trigger = {
				trigger_if = {
					limit = { exists = involved_activity }
					NOT = {
						involved_activity = { has_activity_type = activity_hunt }
					}
				}
				sword_unique_gfx_trigger = no
			}			
			animations_props = marshal_prop
			animations = AI_vengeful_decal
		}

		portrait_modifier = { # Hunting
			trigger = {
				involved_activity ?= { has_activity_type = activity_hunt }
				sword_unique_gfx_trigger = no
			}			
			animations_props = ep2_hunting_sword_right_attachment
			animations = AI_vengeful_decal
		}

		portrait_modifier = { # Equipped
			trigger = {
				any_equipped_character_artifact = { artifact_type = sword }
			}
			animations_props = artifact_sword_equipped_prop
			animations = AI_vengeful_decal
		}

	}
	female = male
	girl = male
	boy = male
}
